## 进入工作单资料登记记录修改页面

1. 请求方式：POST；<br/>
2. URL：/hallworkrequestController/datumView；<br/>
3. 请求示例：http://localhost:9999/hallworkrequestController/datumView<br/>
4. 请求参数：

```
{
    "gzdid":"工作单id 5651021",
    "sydw":"使用单位代码 618840984"
}
```

## 资料登记时查看待检设备列表


1. 请求方式：POST；<br/>
2. URL：/hallworkrequestController/waitingInspection3/{pageNow}/{pageSize}；<br/>
3. 请求示例：http://localhost:9999/hallworkrequestController/waitingInspection3/1/2<br/>

4. 请求参数：

```

{
    "sydwdm":"使用单位代码",
    "sbzl":"设备种类"
}

```

## 获取技术资料

1.请求方式：GET；<br/>
2.请求路径：/hallworkrequestController/findScienceData<br/>
3.请求示例：http://localhost:9999/hallworkrequestController/findScienceData?sbzl=3000<br/>
4.请求参数：

```
sbzl : 设备种类
```

5.响应：

```
{
  "data": [
    {
      "id": "1921",
      "sbzl": "3000",
      "jynr": "1034",
      "xmbh": "16    项目编号",

      "sfbx": "1    是否必需提供(0,否;1,是)",
      "jynrmc": "验收检验    检验内容名称",
      "xl": "    项类",
      "bz": "    备注"
    },
    {
      "id": "1920",
      "sbzl": "3000",
      "jynr": "1034",
      "xmbh": "15",
      "zlmc": "人行道制动距离计算及其修正的计算数据",

      "zlmc": "（1）制造许可证明文件（含明细表）",
      "sfbx": "1",
      "jynrmc": null,
      "xl": "1.1制造资料",
      "bz": null
    }
  ],
  "code": 200,
  "msg": "成功",
  "success": true,
  "list": null,
  "newlist": null,
  "produ": null,
  "map": null,

```

## 技术资料登记,监检

1. 请求方式：POST；<br/>
2. URL：/hallworkrequestController/scienceDataSave<br/>
3. 请求示例:http://localhost:9999/hallworkrequestController/scienceDataSave<br/>
4. 请求参数：

```
[
    {
    "zlmc":"资料名称(xt_jszl表中id) 必须",
    "zlfs":"资料份数",
    "tgqk":"提供情况 长度为1 ",
    "bz":"备注",
    "sbzcdm":"设备注册代码，多个已逗号拼接，xxx111,111xxx 必须"，
    "sydwdm":"使用单位代码",
    "sbzl":"3000 设备种类"
}，
{
    "zlmc":"资料名称(xt_jszl表中id) 必须",
    "zlfs":"资料份数",
    "tgqk":"提供情况 长度为1 ",
    "bz":"备注",
    "sbzcdm":"设备注册代码，多个已逗号拼接，xxx111,111xxx 必须"，
    "sydwdm":"使用单位代码 必须",
    "sbzl":"3000 设备种类 必须"
}
]
```

zlmc：资料名称：https://gitee.com/preeminent_information/dashboard/wikis/preeminent_information%2Fdata_registration?doc_id=304582&sort_id=1449264<br/>
对应 "id": "1921"<br/>

5. 响应：

```
{
  "data": [
    {
      "id": "1488826",
      "gzdid": null,
      "zlmc": null,
      "zlfs": null,
      "jsr": "",
      "jssj": "2019-05-13",
      "tgqk": null,
      "bz": null,
      "type": "1",
      "sbzcdm": "30134403002005010312"
    },
    {
      "id": "1488827",
      "gzdid": null,
      "zlmc": null,
      "zlfs": null,
      "jsr": "",
      "jssj": "2019-05-13",
      "tgqk": null,
      "bz": null,
      "type": "1",
      "sbzcdm": "Q8108888882009Y00043"
    }
  ],
  "code": 200,
  "msg": "成功",
  "success": true,
  "list": null,
  "newlist": null,
  "produ": null,
  "map": null,
  "object": null
}
```

## 技术资料登记,监检 驳回
1. 请求方式：POST；<br/>
2. URL：/hallworkrequestController/scienceDataBack<br/>
3. 请求示例：http://localhost:9999/hallworkrequestController/scienceDataBack<br/>
4. 请求参数：

```
[
	{
	"sbzcdm":"30134403002005010312 设备注册代码",
	"id":"1488824 资料登记id，https://gitee.com/preeminent_information/dashboard/wikis/preeminent_information%2Fdata_registration?doc_id=304582&sort_id=1449937 返回的id"
	},
	{
	"sbzcdm":"Q8108888882009Y00043",
	"id":"1488825"
	}
]
```

5. 响应：

```
{
  "data": null,
  "code": 200,
  "msg": "成功",
  "success": true,
  "list": null,
  "newlist": null,
  "produ": null,
  "map": null,
  "object": null
}
```
